***натыкающийся.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:натыкающийся.html>натыка́ющийся</a> (9890)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:натягивать.html>натя́гивать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">natjágivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:натягиваться.html>натя́гиваться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">natjágivatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:натянуться.html>натяну́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to stretch, to be or become taut or elastic
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кожа.html>ко́жа</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:натягиваться.html>натя́гивается</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:скула.html>ску́лах</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kóža <b>natjágivajetsja</b> na skúlax</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the skin <b>stretches/is stretched</b> over the cheekbones</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:натягивать.html>натя́гивать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">natjágivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тянуть.html>тяну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tjanútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:натянуть.html>натяну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">natjanútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:натягивать.html>натя́гивать</a></b>)

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:натянуть.html>натяну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">natjanútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:натянуться.html>натяну́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">natjanútʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:натягиваться.html>натя́гиваться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to stretch, to be or become taut or elastic
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кожа.html>ко́жа</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:натянуться.html>натяну́лась</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:скула.html>ску́лах</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kóža <b>natjanúlasʹ</b> na skúlax</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the skin (was) <b>stretched</b> over the cheekbones</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:натянуть.html>натяну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">natjanútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***наугад.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наугад.html>науга́д</a> (9496)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">угад(а́ть)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ugad(átʹ)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наугад.html>науга́д</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">naugád</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>at random</li>
<li>by guesswork</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<ol><li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="<a href = vnd.unilang:философский.html>филосо́фское</a>">филос.</span> сфера человеческой деятельности, имеющая целью сбор, накопление, классификацию, анализ, обобщение, передачу и использование фактов, построение теорий, позволяющих адекватно описывать природные или общественные (<i>гуманитарные науки</i>) процессы и прогнозировать их развитие <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">Он занимается <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">наукой</span>. </span> <span class="example-fullblock"></li>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">Вернувшись в Ленинград, он с головой ушёл в <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">науку</span>. </span></li>
</ul></li>


<li>система знаний, полученных в результате этой деятельности и составляющих научную картину мира <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black"><span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">Наука</span> утверждает, что скорость света конечна. </span></li>
</ul></li>


<li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="<a href = vnd.unilang:устаревший.html>устаре́вшее</a>">устар.</span> нечто поучительное, позволяющее сделать важные выводы для изменения поведения человека <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">Поделом тебе, старый невежа! // Впредь тебе, невежа, <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">наука</span>. </span></li>
</ul></li>


</ol>

***научиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:научиться.html>научи́ться</a> (1897)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:научить.html>научи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">naučítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:научиться.html>научи́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">naučítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:учиться.html>учи́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>(+ dative case) to learn <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">implying that an individual or a group starts to learn something all by itself with the intention of full accomplishment</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наш.html>на́ша</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:команда.html>кома́нда</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мо́жет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:многое.html>мно́гому</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:научиться.html>научи́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:противостояние.html>противостоя́нии</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Náša kománda móžet mnógomu <b>naučítʹsja</b> v protivostojánii.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Our team can learn a lot in the confrontation.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наука.html>нау́ка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">naúka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ухо.html>у́хо</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">úxo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ник</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наушник.html>нау́шник</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">naúšnik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наушник.html>нау́шника</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наушник.html>нау́шники</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наушник.html>нау́шников</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">radio</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> headphone, earphone</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic<span class="ib-comma">,</span> slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> earflap</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> informer, telltale; slanderer <span class="defdate">[from 18th c.]</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нахальство.html>наха́льство</a> (15681)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жало.html>наха́л</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">naxál</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ство</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-stvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нахальство.html>наха́льство</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">naxálʹstvo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нахальство.html>наха́льства</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нахальство.html>наха́льства</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нахальство.html>наха́льств</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>impudence, insolence, impertinence, effrontery, sauce, cheek
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:иметь.html>име́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нахальство.html>наха́льство</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">imétʹ <b>naxálʹstvo</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to have the impudence/cheek <i>(to)</i>; have the face <i>(to)</i></span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хлынуть.html>хлы́нуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xlýnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
